< review>
Jeanne and her staff were very kind and informative.  They helped me with any questions I had and worked hard to help me find the engagement ring I wanted.   I was very happy that they let me do it my way, answering my questions and being supportive without being pushy or trying to give me their "sales pitch".   I had a rough idea of what I wanted and what kind of information I needed, and at many other places I found it hard to get through the process in the driver's seat, so to speak.   Other places were always trying to sell me on a certain ring or a certain philosophy - Jeanne and her staff at The Classic Rock were far better at just being supportive and informative when I had questions, but more importantly also give me space take my time and think about my decision, and to look at the stones as I chose.   They also had a microscope setup that I used regularly which was very convenient (some other places don't have that).  Overall very informative, very honest and very helpful.  5 stars!!< /review>

< text>
After several months I am finally writing this review for this amazing establishment.  I came here, with my girlfiend, around July to attend the diamond class that they offer.  I literally knew nothing when it came to diamonds (they all sort of looked the same to me) but Shawn was very diligent in informing us about the basics of diamonds and how they are categorized.  She tailored the lesson as we went along to discuss topics that we had more interest in.  It really felt like a class!  We compared sizes, colors and clarity of diamonds and she brings out examples to compare, giving us a clearer picture of the topics she was explaining.  The class itself is very in depth and informative, it ultimately helped me make a choice for my purchase of an engagement ring.

I came back a few months later in September I emailed The Classic Rock and made an appointment to come in, hoping to get the process started on choosing an engagement ring within the one hour I had prior to work.  The staff is very welcoming and attentive to all of your ideas and requests, as well as your time constraints!  Ruth had brought up the information that was written down during the diamond class we took in July so it was easy to choose a round cut, but she helped me decide what diamond size range I wanted to go with.  After this visit they had ordered a few diamonds that fit the criteria we discussed within my one hour visit.

A few days later the diamonds arrive and I am again at the store deciding between carat weights of the selected diamonds that fit the criteria I chose.  It was such a simple process as Ruth, Shawn and Jeanne provide input on all the pro's and cons between the diamonds in terms of different aspects of the diamonds themselves.  I thought I'd have a little more stress in this choosing process but it was so simple coming here. I went with a 1.51 carat VS2 F clarity round cut!  I cannot stress how simple it was to get this process started and for them to work around my time constraints and take into consideration my budget.  My ring was basically done; my diamond was chosen, the band was chosen and I just had one last request.  I wanted to add a little detail to the band and requested to place a small sapphire stone on one side of the band so only she could see it.  Ruth took the request and made it happen!  She gave an example of the finished product while the ring was being put together and I was overly satisfied with the result.

Fast forward 4-6 weeks in October later and the ring was finished.  I pretended to go to the gym but I really picked up the ring!  Fast forward again to November at the Conservatory of Flowers in SF where I proposed to my girlfriend.  She said yes of course!  All thanks to The Classic Rock.  I still cannot believe how easy they made it for me to choose a ring.  I highly recommend this place to any guy looking to purchase an engagement ring.  I promise it isn't as scary as you'd think, as long as you come here!</text>

< text>

< review>
I was out for my evening walk and decided to get some quick food to munch on. I ended up at Wingstop near PCC. I was greeted by a friendly hello as I entered the store. All the covid-19 protocols posted on the door were being followed. I gave the girl my order and stepped outside to wait for it to be prepared. I ordered a selection of boneless chicken wings... Garlic parmesan and mango habanero. I also decided it was time to try their fresh cut fries again.

When the food was ready, she motioned for me to come inside. And I was on my way home.

All of the food was good and was perfect to munch on, while watching a movie on TV. Great flavor and texture with the chicken wings. The fresh cut fries were excellent!

While the inside is closed for sit down, they do have a table or two out front. There is street parking, as well as a parking lot in the back of this shopping area.

I will definitely be back again... I want to try some of the other sides.

P.S.... I ordered the boneless chicken combo at Liela's suggestion ... Wings, fries, and drink... All for just over 10 bucks. Good value..<//review>

< text>
What a great place. I walked into the shop. Now I only have fishing setups for steurgion, stripper. But didn't have a setup for salmon. Now I know a little about fishing so I top Rick, just set me up with something good. So he looked at 6 different rods and when he felt that he had 2 that were just about right he handed them to me and said feel these 2 and tell which one you would pick. G Loomis  was the pick. Now the reel. Shamono in know was the choice and he pick one with a deep spool setup just in case I got a runner. Loaded it up with so 30lb braid line and I was done. Went out fishing right after purchase first drift 30 salmon in the boat. 2nd drift 10 lb salmon in the boat. Rod felt great, reel was smooth , and the line really connected me to where I could feel what the fish was doing and heading. Exelent service. Thank you rick.<//text>

Samsara In sanskrit means endless cycle of life, death and rebirth. They definitely give their grapes a rebirth with all their wine. This is the 1st and only wine tasting room in Goleta so far. Their tasting menu usually has one white and rest are red and recently included  a Rose as well. Their staff are very knowledgeable, especially Devon (I love how he enunciates his words) and Claudia, she is a newer member but just as friendly and knowledgeable and will provide a lot of information on each wine they pour. <time>1562626604323</time><Rating>5</Rating><text>I recently discovered SAMsARA Wine Co.'s Goleta Winery and Tasting Room and have had a number of excellent experiences there already.

First off, their wine is top notch.  I am a big fan of Santa Barbara County Pinot Noirs, Syrahs, Grenaches and Chardonnays, so I was really excited to discover that this is their exact wheelhouse.  From their single vineyard offerings to their multi-vineyard blends, I was thoroughly impressed.

Second, the tasting experience was really relaxed and pleasant.  My group was not in a rush and the staff members not only picked up on that, but encouraged us to take our time and enjoy the afternoon.  They also engaged each member of our group, regardless of how much each person knew about wine, which really made it special for the newbies.

Lastly, they have a great location.  Just a few turns off the freeway, with plenty of parking, and in the same business park as Captain Fatty's Brewery, I'll be back again soon!</text>< pictures>

Pizza by the slice...nothing more, nothing less. Pretty decent and affordable place in the neighborhood to grab a slice after a boozy night. THE NOT SO GOOD:

Cold pizza
not cooked enough
Vegetarian pizza is a joke

I have a three car garage. One two car door and a single car door. My two car garage door circa 1999 jammed internally and not having proper working over current protection proceeded to consume it self. It being  Saturday am I called the phone number on the tag by the opener. Hours later still no response. I googled Garage door repair, picked Heritage for being local and well rated. They came almost immediately and got the door closed. We discussed various options. Decided on new door and two new openers. They guaranteed to match the small door. They came as scheduled did the install and everything was fine...almost. The new door was slightly less white than the old door. They had promised to match exactly....Neither of us had noticed the old garage doors had been painted. After a couple days of negotiating Heritage decided the best solution was to replace the small door.  This they did quickly and as efficiently as the first door. I know this is long, but the entire story needed telling to demonstrate the lengths Heritage will go for customer satisfaction. I know without a doubt if I ever have garage door problems all I need do is call Heritage and they will respond quickly and professionally and resolve my problem.<//review>

<text>First, let me premise this review with my years patronizing VIP Tint.  I had been using VIP Tint for all my auto tint needs for more than 15 years.  Despite leaving the area and residing in various counties (San Bernardino, San Diego, and Riverside), I still bring all my vehicles to VIP Tint in Temecula/Murrieta.
On 13 January 2020, I made a 0900 appointment for (yet) another vehicle.  When I spoke with the owner, he was unable to afford me any discount on my tints so I decided to forego my headlight protector.  It was going to cost a great deal of money for my daily car.  After a few minutes, he offered a $25 discount so I could avail of this protector.  The films were already cut for my vehicle anyway.  Hence, whether I get it today or some other time, he stated that the film will just be laying around.  To assist and ease the owner of his trouble, I decided to grab the opportunity.
After an hour or so, another customer came for a set of tint‚Äîsimilar to mine.  He was offered $10 difference from my quote.  He had a Mercedes crossover‚Äîlarger than my 4-door sedan.  In my mind I thought they could not afford me any discount but here you go, another customer came by and received the discounted price for the tints.  I had to give them the benefit of the doubt hoping they will honor the same quote for my car.
Nevertheless, when I was about to pay for my tints, a Caucasian male employee with long white (gray) beard, informed me that I was not going to get the same price but only a $5 discount.  I informed him to bill me the initial amount.  To my amaze, he was hostile, uncouth, unprofessional, and curt. <Review>I originally went to The Rink only monthly for Sac City Rollers roller derby bouts but I just went last night for their Sunday 7-9:30p open skate session and had a great time and will be coming back for more before they temporarily shut down for roof maintenance summer 2017.

Excellent music selection and requests are free. Open and welcoming staff members and patrons. It's hard to beat $5.50 for 2.5hrs of skating! Open and free parking and is handicap accessible.

The only two qualms I have with The Rink is, one, their floor - not a traditional wooden, which isn't a deal breaker, but it has seen some damage that they've attempted to fix but leaves for a textured skating surface compared to other rinks in the area. Second item of note is for when I'm photographing roller derby bouts - the giant bright orange "The Rink" on the big wall is hideous and makes for terrible photographing.< /Review><Gmap_id>0x809adcbe9ef6195b:0x79aa65b2db7f2c32< /Gmap_id>< user>

<user_id>113839548270144399394< /user_id><gmap_id>0x809adcbe9ef6195b:0x79aa65b2db7f2c32< /gmap_id><pics>None<//pics>< Text>
I went to The Rink this past weekend and woah... Woah, is all that I really have to say about this place. The outside seems ran down, and it's not exactly in the best area. I decided to go to The Rink because my friends were interested in trying out a skating rink in the area. I guess a plus, would be that it's not the hardest place to find. Parking in the parking lot is okay. The parking lot when I arrived was full of around 30-40 cars, but seemed dirty. There was cups all over the parking lot, and trash scattered. I didn't let a dirty parking lot ruin the night of fun that was about to happen. We went inside the lobby area, and I have no complaints. Was easy and pretty quick to get inside seeing as there was a line of around 15 people, they did actually get us in pretty quick. Once inside I went to their skate rack to find a pair of skates. Woah, that's the next ting! The person working at their skate counter was absolutely rude, I asked for a size 8, and it was too small. I went up to the counter to exchange the pair of skates for a size nine and they called me and idiot! Are you serious?  I got the wrong size skate so I'm an idiot.. Isn't that just what I wanted to hear today.. He said it to a buddy quietly as he was turning around, but I was able to hear. Throughout the night all I really did was skate with my friends. As much skating as we could do with all of the punk kids skating way too fast, and way too close to us. They were extremely rude and didn't care about anyone in their way. There was absolutely no enforcement of any type of safety rules, and the music they were playing was absolutely horrible for a public place. I will never be back.</Text>
